## Pending

- [ ] [HIGH] [anon] Home `/` "CURRENTLY FEATURED" stat block stamps Survivor with `June 2026 CANON REVISED`, but the deeper `/shows/survivor` page header ŌĆö the same canonical fact about the same show ŌĆö stamps `May 2026 CANON REVISED`. A first-time reader who clicks through from home to the show in the same minute sees two different last-revised dates for the same canon. Source: `src/lib/canon/last-revised.ts:46-51` documents the divergence directly ŌĆö `getCanonRevisedLabel(now = new Date())` derives the home's label from build time, while `canonRevisedLabelFromIso(iso)` (called from `src/app/shows/[show]/page.tsx:176` via the canon's actual `last_revised` frontmatter) derives the show page's. The comment even calls the home value a "freshness signal' derived from build time" ŌĆö but the **label** still says "CANON REVISED" which reads as a factual editorial claim, not a build-time signal. This undercuts the trust the canon is built on; the home page is the public surface that promises the editorial work, and stamping a build-month label as if it were the canon's revision month is the brand-central place to be honest. The drift will become visible on the 1st of every month (today, 2026-06-01, is the first day it's flipped ŌĆö the build that ran tonight stamps June while the canon was last touched in May), and every month after. Fix options (pick one): (a) derive the home `Canon revised` label from the featured show's actual `canon.last_revised` (the canonical fix ŌĆö sources match, label remains accurate; requires reading the featured show's canon at home-page build time, which is already loaded for the featured-card path); (b) rename the home label from `Canon revised` to `Last refreshed` or `Site refreshed` so the build-month signal is honest about being a build signal, not a canon date; (c) drop the home stat row's `CANON REVISED` cell entirely and rely on the show-page hero stat for the fact (smallest blast radius ŌĆö the home keeps the `50 SEASONS RANKED` cell intact). Recommended: (a) ŌĆö both surfaces agree, the editorial promise is preserved, and the home's freshness signal stays accurate because canon revisions outpace build cadence in steady state anyway. Pin with a colocated test on the home featured-card or `HomeHero` that mounts the component against a fixture show with `canon.last_revised = '2026-05-15'` and asserts the rendered stamp reads `May 2026`, not the current month; bonus invariant in `scripts/content-check.ts` that for the featured show, the home's `Canon revised` source path matches the show page's source path (both reading `canon.last_revised`). Spoiler discipline P0 unchanged (date format only). (URL: /, source: critique-pass-24)

- [ ] [MED] [anon] `/sign-in` page `<meta name="description">` reads `Sign in to tiered. Magic link by email.` ŌĆö the brand has been truncated to `tiered.` (dropping the `.tv` suffix). CLAUDE.md hard rule 6 is explicit: "The brand name is `tiered.tv` ŌĆö always lowercase, including the `.tv` suffix. Never capitalize the T. The dot is part of the wordmark; never stylize, color, or kern it apart." A description of `Sign in to tiered.` puts a fullstop where the `.tv` belongs, which reads as if the brand name ends mid-word ŌĆö the literal opposite of the brand-mark contract. The route is `noIndex: true` so search engines won't surface this in SERP snippets, but the description still ships in the rendered head and is visible to (a) any social/preview crawler that ignores `noIndex` for inspection, (b) a reader using View Source, (c) the OG/Twitter card fallback path that pulls from `<meta description>` when an explicit OG description is absent. Source: `src/app/(default)/sign-in/page.tsx`'s `buildMetadata({ description: 'Sign in to tiered. Magic link by email.', path: '/sign-in', noIndex: true })`. Fix: change the description literal to `Sign in to tiered.tv. Magic link by email.` ŌĆö the dot before `tv` is part of the brand wordmark, not the sentence-ending fullstop. Pin with a colocated test in `src/app/(default)/sign-in/__tests__/page.test.tsx` asserting the description string includes the literal substring `tiered.tv` (the unit gate would catch any future authoring pass that re-truncated the suffix); bonus invariant ŌĆö extend the existing `scripts/content-check.ts` brand-spelling check (if any; otherwise add one) that scans every `description` string returned from a `buildMetadata` call across the route tree and rejects any value matching `\btiered\.\s*(?!tv)` (a stray `tiered.` not followed by `tv`). Spoiler discipline P0 unchanged (metadata text edit only). (URL: /sign-in, source: critique-pass-24)

- [ ] [MED] [anon] `/shows/survivor` "What changed this week" panel renders position diffs (`was #08 now #44`, `36 this week`) under an eyebrow that reads `UPDATED THURSDAY` ŌĆö but the panel never labels which ranking is shifting. The panel sits **above** the canon/community tab pair, and is followed by the editorial copy block that names the canon as "one ranking, written by editors ŌĆ” revised quarterly when a new season changes the math." A first-time reader scanning vertically reads: weekly-shifting movers panel ŌåÆ canon/community tab toggle ŌåÆ "revised quarterly" promise ŌĆö and is left to infer that a panel showing 36-slot weekly moves belongs to the community side. The visual proximity to the canon eyebrow invites the wrong inference (an editorial canon that moved 36 slots in a week would directly contradict the "revised quarterly" promise that renders one screen below). The previous pass-23 finding on this surface trimmed `SENTIMENT-TAGGED` from the eyebrow but didn't add the source-of-truth label the panel still owes. Fix options: (a) extend the eyebrow to read `WHAT CHANGED IN THE COMMUNITY RANK ┬Ę UPDATED THURSDAY` (or `COMMUNITY RANK ┬Ę UPDATED THURSDAY`) ŌĆö names the source explicitly without lengthening the panel; (b) move the existing `community rank updates weekly` microcopy from the season-page VotePair into this panel's footer, so the source-of-truth caption sits inside the same visual scope as the deltas; (c) restructure so the panel sits *below* the tab pair on the community-active pane and is absent on the canon-active pane (largest blast radius ŌĆö touches the tab-toggle state machine). The qualifier `on the season itself` reads as if there is somewhere else one could weigh in on something other than the season (the show? the canon slot? the franchise?). On a season page where the entire thread is scoped to that season, `itself` does not earn its place ŌĆö it reads slightly arch, in the same voice-violation class as the pass-23 `SENTIMENT-TAGGED` finding ("plain sentences over clever ones"). Two clean trims: (a) `No comments yet. Be the first to weigh in.` (positive CTA, peer voice), or (b) `No comments yet. Open the thread.` (action-oriented, terse). Recommended: (a) ŌĆö the "be the first to" frame echoes how the authed user is already invited to participate elsewhere on the page (the CAST VOTE button reads as the same kind of invitation), and matches the welcoming-peer register the bearings voice cue names. Locate: `CommentThreadLive.tsx` or the comment-thread empty-state composition that renders alongside `CommentInput` in the authed branch. Pin: colocated test asserting the empty-state text contains `Be the first to weigh in` and does not contain `/itself/i` (regression pin against the awkward qualifier). Spoiler discipline P0 unchanged (copy edit only). (URL: /shows/survivor/season/heroes-vs-villains, source: critique-pass-23)

- [x] [LOW] [anon] The `/shows/[show]` canon/community tab control (`src/components/canon/CanonTabSwitch.tsx`) renders each tab as `<span class="cp-tab-marker">01</span><span><span class="cp-tab-name">Editor's Canon</span><span class="cp-tab-cap">curated</span></span>` ŌĆö the name and the state cap are adjacent inline spans with no whitespace or separator between them, and the `<button role="tab">` carries no `aria-label`. On desktop the two read as a single run-together token (`Editor's Canoncurated`, `Communitylive`); on mobile CSS line-breaks the cap so it separates. The button's accessible name therefore computes to `01Editor's Canoncurated` / `02Communitylive`, which a screen reader announces as one mashed token. Evidence: desktop capture text `01 / Editor's CanonCURATED / 02 / CommunityLIVE` vs mobile `01 / Editor's Canon / CURATED`. - [x] [HIGH] [anon] /shows nine of thirteen show taglines close on the identical "Ranked without <verb> a single <noun>." template ŌĆö read top-to-bottom on the tier-list page the repeating clause scans as fill-in-the-blank generation, not a knowledgeable peer writing per show. Verified on disk via grep: Drag Race ("Ranked without spoiling a single crowning."), Love Island UK ("...final couple."), GBBO/Bake Off ("...Star Baker."), Project Runway ("...finale collection."), Bachelorette ("...hometown."), Love Island US ("...recoupling."), The Challenge ("...elimination."), Bachelor ("Ranked without giving away a single final rose."), Big Brother ("Ranked without ruining a single eviction."). Top Chef has no such tag; Amazing Race uses a different shape ("We've ranked every leg of every one"); Survivor's tagline is longer-form. The inconsistency makes the repeating nine stand out more, not less. The site-wide "No spoilers" promise is already carried structurally by the chrome (header + footer `<ShieldBadge>` + the home-page brand promise) ŌĆö every per-show repetition is editorial dead weight. Fix: drop the trailing "Ranked without <verb> a single <noun>." clause from at least six of the nine offenders and let each show's tagline close on its own editorial observation, the way Top Chef and Amazing Race already do. The clause's content is already covered site-wide; the tagline space is editorial real estate that should land an idea unique to that show. Pin with a `scripts/content-check.ts` invariant (laxŌåÆstrict in the existing `STRICT` / `CROSS_SHOW_STRICT` / `YEAR_TENURE_STRICT` pattern) asserting at most N shows carry the templated trailing clause (initial floor: Ōēż 3; final strict floor: Ōēż 1) ŌĆö same shape as the cross-show-coverage and year-tenure invariants already in place. Spoiler discipline P0 unchanged ŌĆö editorial-voice rewrite only. (URL: /shows, every show home-page card surface that quotes the tagline, source: critique-pass-12) ŌĆö 60abb0d ŌĆö issue #187 ŌĆö RESOLVED at c4f0e6c: content-curator rewrote all ten offenders (the nine the critique named plus Traitors, which uses the same template ŌĆö "Ranked without naming a single traitor."). Nine had the trailing clause dropped outright; each tagline now closes on the editorial observation already present in the penultimate sentence (Bachelorette ŌåÆ "warmer, sharper, and more willing to let the lead drive."; Bachelor ŌåÆ "running uninterrupted since 2002."; Love Island UK ŌåÆ "summer and winter editions included."; Project Runway ŌåÆ "still the one to beat."; Bake Off ŌåÆ "and somehow the most watchable."; The Challenge ŌåÆ "the genre's true combat league."; Traitors ŌåÆ "faster than anyone expected."; Love Island US ŌåÆ "finally found its footing on Peacock."). Drag Race was rebuilt as a two-sentence tagline matching siblings: "17 seasons of queens at a Los Angeles workroom, sewing through mini-challenges and lip-syncing for their lives on a pink-lit runway. The format that built a global drag economy and still sets the bar every other franchise chases." Big Brother extended the existing closer with a clause ("ŌĆ”and still the loudest room on summer television") rather than ending on the fragmentary "invented the genre.". Pinned with `scripts/content-check.ts` `collectTaglineTemplatedTailIssues()` + new `TAGLINE_TAIL_STRICT = true` toggle ŌĆö strict floor 0, because the rewrite drained every offender in one tick (skipped the lax intermediate per the critique's "laxŌåÆstrict in the STRICT / CROSS_SHOW_STRICT / YEAR_TENURE_STRICT pattern" guidance ŌĆö no daylight to keep). Eight colocated tests in `src/content/__tests__/content-check.test.ts` pin the regex shape across the four verb forms (spoiling / ruining / naming / giving away), the multi-word noun phrases (final couple, Star Baker, finale collection), the legal "Ranked by ŌĆ”" sibling (Top Chef), the legal "We have ranked every single one" sibling (Survivor / Amazing Race), and a live-catalog integration check reading zero offenders against the production content tree. - [x] [MED] [anon] On `/shows/survivor/season/heroes-vs-villains` the "WHAT TO WATCH FOR" ŌåÆ "LATE ┬Ę THIRD ACT" callout body reads `The cold-open of the late-game stretch is doing real ethnographic labor ŌĆö staging, blocking, who's eating where. Underlying cause: some season `title:` fields are real names ("Heroes vs. Villains", "Winners at War", "Las Vegas") while others are bare "Season N" (e.g. `content/shows/dragrace/seasons/06-season-6.md`, `content/shows/amazing-race/seasons/07-season-7.md`). Fix: pick one rule for the secondary label across all `/themes/<list>/` rows and apply consistently ŌĆö either always show the editorialized name (fill in the missing season titles in the source content) or always strip to bare "SEASON N" in `season_label`. Drop The Traitors' parenthetical year ŌĆö no other entry asks for it. Sweep all 12 `content/themes/*.md` for the same pattern. (URL: /themes/best-finales, source: critique-pass-8) ŌĆö 6b81691 ŌĆö issue #161 ŌĆö RESOLVED at 025e601: 17 edits across 10 `content/themes/*.md` files stripped every `S<NN> ┬Ę Season N` and `S<NN> ┬Ę Season N (YYYY)` `season_label` to the bare `S<NN>` form (the `S<NN>` prefix already names the season number, so the subtitle was redundant; the parenthetical year was the same class plus an ornament no other entry asks for). - [x] [MED] [authed] scripts/critique-walk.mjs captures page innerText immediately after the `load` event, before client auth islands hydrate ŌĆö the authed pass-2 walk produced two false-positive HIGH auth-state findings; the walk should settle for network-idle / island hydration before capture (URL: n/a, source: critique-pass-2) ŌĆö issue #125 ŌĆö RESOLVED this commit: `walk()` navigated with `page.goto(target, { waitUntil: 'load' })` and captured `document.body.innerText` immediately ŌĆö before the header auth-state island (`HeaderView`) had run its mount `useEffect`, which fetches `GET /api/auth/me` and only then re-renders the chrome between signed-out and signed-in. So the authed walk read the pre-hydration SSR DOM ("Sign in"), filing false-positive HIGH auth-state findings (two withdrawn in pass 2; a third authed observation ŌĆö the season comment composer reading "Sign in to comment" against a `@e2e / Sign out` header ŌĆö withdrawn in pass 3 precisely because it was indistinguishable from this artifact). Fix: two new exported helpers + a per-page settle. Before navigation the walk arms `page.waitForResponse` for the `/api/auth/me` request (pre-`.catch()`'d so a timeout can't surface as an unhandled rejection while `goto` is still in flight); after the `load`-event `goto` it calls `settleForHydration`, which awaits that response (pinning the one request whose result changes the chrome) then `page.waitForLoadState('networkidle', { timeout: SETTLE_TIMEOUT })` so the island re-render ŌĆö and any other island, e.g. the season comment composer ŌĆö has flushed. Both waits are best-effort: a `networkidle` timeout and an auth-fetch rejection are both swallowed, so a slow page or a chatty third-party beacon delays the capture, never fails it. New `SETTLE_TIMEOUT` (8000ms, exported, `--settle-timeout` override) bounds the worst case under the 20s nav timeout. New pure export `isAuthMeRequest(url)` ŌĆö pathname-exact `/api/auth/me` match, origin/query agnostic, no throw on a non-URL ŌĆö is the `waitForResponse` predicate. ┬¦5a: 7 new colocated tests in `scripts/__tests__/critique-walk.test.mjs` ŌĆö `SETTLE_TIMEOUT` shape, `isAuthMeRequest` (matches with/without query + cross-origin, rejects sibling endpoints + sub-paths, non-URL ŌåÆ false no throw), `settleForHydration` (awaits auth then networkidle in that order, swallows a networkidle timeout, swallows an auth-response rejection and still runs the idle wait, handles the pre-caught null shape). No new URL or page family ŌĆö a change to the critique tooling, not the product ŌĆö so no e2e fixture row. Verify green: leg1 tokens + typecheck + no-raw-img + unit + 99 script tests + content:check (13 shows/298 seasons/13 canons/12 themes/3 legal docs), leg2 build, leg3 1319 e2e.

Lax-mode failure, same shape as the canon-heading rule from #66. Labels with no separator (e.g. a bare "S41") and entries with no `season_label` at all stay legal. Colocated tests cover the failure case, the passing case, the no-separator and no-label tolerances, a multi-word season title (`Heroes vs. Villains`), and the referential-error preservation (unknown-show still surfaces).

- [x] [MED] [anon] /themes, /themes/[theme] ŌĆö "cross-canon" copy overpromises against an all-Survivor catalog (URL: /themes, /themes/[theme], source: critique-pass-1) ŌĆö issue #98 ŌĆö RESOLVED this commit: `ListsHero` and `AdjacentLists` are now coverage-aware. `ListsHero` derives both the H1 accent and the lede from `stats.showsCovered`: when Ōēź2 shows are covered it keeps the current "Cross-canon." accent + "Some span every show. Some live inside one." lede; when exactly 1 show is covered (today's reality at 12 lists / 1 show) it switches to "Inside one canon." + "Every list lives inside one canon today ŌĆö cross-canon entries arrive as more catalogues fill in." `AdjacentLists.tagFor` now checks the *other* theme's actual show-coverage on the cross-category branch: when the other list spans only one show, the qualifier drops from "cross-canon list" to "<category> list" (e.g. "Ōå® single-show list" / "single-show list Ōå¬"); the genuine cross-canon-list label survives only when the other list truly spans Ōēź2 shows. New `data-coverage` attribute on the hero (`cross-canon|single-canon`) and two new locks: a single-canon `ListsHero` test asserts the accent + lede swap, and a cross-category `AdjacentLists` test asserts the "cross-canon" label survives only on a multi-show fixture. - [x] [needs-user-call] reader-driven critique was not auth-isolatable in either direction ŌĆö RESOLVED 2026-05-19 (oversight): pass 1 proved the `reader` sub-agent drives the operator's real, shared Chrome profile and had no cookie primitive, so its "anon" walk inherited the operator's live session (false HIGH filed + withdrawn) and its authed walk could not run. **Fix applied (user-approved, option 1):** `.claude/agents/reader.md` now carries `mcp__claude-in-chrome__javascript_tool` and a mandatory Step 0 that *deterministically* clears cookies + verifies `/api/auth/me ŌåÆ signedIn:false` for the anon pass and sets `__session` + verifies `signedIn:true` for the authed pass, exiting `auth-failed` rather than walking a contaminated profile. `plan/bearings.md` "Working harness contract" rewritten ŌĆö reliability is now structural (verify-or-exit gate), not incidental profile luck. **Separate open question** (raised by user 2026-05-19, not a blocker for the above): whether `/critique` should also run in GitHub Actions, not just local ŌĆö see the oversight summary; that needs a headless-browser reader path and is a phase-candidate decision, tracked outside this row.
